for I know not the numbers thereof. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> I will go in the strength of the Lord GOD: I will make mention of thy righteousness, even of thine only. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> O God, thou hast taught me from my youth: and hitherto have I declared thy wondrous works. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Now also when I am old and grayheaded, O God, forsake me not; until I have shewed thy strength unto this generation, and thy power to every one that is to come.^[**71:18** when…: Heb. unto old age and gray hairs]^[**71:18** thy strength: Heb. thine arm] <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Thy righteousness also, O God, is very high, who hast done great things: O God, who is like unto thee! <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Thou, which hast shewed me great and sore troubles, shalt quicken me again, and shalt bring me up again from the depths of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Thou shalt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every side. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> I will also praise thee with the psaltery, even thy truth, O my God: unto thee will I sing with the harp, O thou Holy One of Israel.^[**71:22** the psaltery: Heb. the instrument of psaltery] <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing unto thee; and my soul, which thou hast redeemed. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the day long: for they are confounded, for they are brought unto shame, that seek my hurt.




 

# 72 
A Psalm for Solomon. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Give the king thy judgments, O God, and thy righteousness unto the king’s son.^[**72:1** for: or, of] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> He shall judge thy people with righteousness, and thy poor with judgment. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the little hills, by righteousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> He shall judge the poor of the people, he shall save the children of the needy, and shall break in pieces the oppressor. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They shall fear thee as long as the sun and moon endure, throughout all generations. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass: as showers that water the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> In his days shall the righteous flourish; and abundance of peace so long as the moon endureth.^[**72:7** so long…: Heb. till there be no moon] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> They that dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him; and his enemies shall lick the dust. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Yea, all kings shall fall down before him: all nations shall serve him. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; the poor also, and him that hath no helper. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> He shall spare the poor and needy, and shall save the souls of the needy. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: and precious shall their blood be in his sight. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: prayer also shall be made for him continually; and daily shall he be praised.^[**72:15** shall be given: Heb. one shall give] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> There shall be an handful of corn in the earth upon the top of the mountains; the fruit thereof shall shake like Lebanon: and they of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> His name shall endure for ever: his name shall be continued as long as the sun: and men shall be blessed in him: all nations shall call him blessed.^[**72:17** endure: Heb. be]^[**72:17** his name shall be…: Heb. shall be as a son to continue his father’s name for ever] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, who only doeth wondrous things. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> And blessed be his glorious name for ever: and let the whole earth be filled with his glory; Amen, and Amen. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.




 

# 73 
A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Truly God is good to Israel, even to such as are of a clean heart.^[**73:1** of: or, for]^[**73:1** Truly: or, Yet]^[**73:1** of…: Heb. clean of heart] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> But as for me, my feet were almost gone; my steps had well nigh slipped. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For I was envious at the foolish, when I saw the prosperity of the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For there are no bands in their death: but their strength is firm.^[**73:4** firm: Heb. fat] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They are not in trouble as other men; neither are they plagued like other men.^[**73:5** in…: Heb. in the trouble of other men]^[**73:5** like: Heb. with] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Therefore pride compasseth them about as a chain; violence covereth them as a garment. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Their eyes stand out with fatness: they have more than heart could wish.^[**73:7** have…: Heb. pass the thoughts of the heart] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> They are corrupt, and speak wickedly concerning oppression: they speak loftily. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> They set their mouth against the heavens, and their tongue walketh through the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Therefore his people return hither: and waters of a full cup are wrung out to them. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> And they say, How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the most High? <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Behold, these are the ungodly, who prosper in the world; they increase in riches. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Verily I have cleansed my heart in vain, and washed my hands in innocency. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> For all the day long have I been plagued, and chastened every morning.^[**73:14** chastened: Heb. my chastisement was] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> If I say, I will speak thus; behold, I should offend against the generation of thy children. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> When I thought to know this, it was too painful for me;^[**73:16** too…: Heb. labour in mine eyes] <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Until I went into the sanctuary of God; then understood I their end. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Surely thou didst set them in slippery places: thou castedst them down into destruction. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> How are they brought into desolation, as in a moment! they are utterly consumed with terrors. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> As a dream when one awaketh; so, O Lord, when thou awakest, thou shalt despise their image. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Thus my heart was grieved, and I was pricked in my reins. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> So foolish was I, and ignorant: I was as a beast before thee.^[**73:22** ignorant: Heb. I knew not]^[**73:22** before: Heb. with] <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Nevertheless I am continually with thee: thou hast holden me by my right hand. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> Thou shalt guide me with thy counsel, and afterward receive me to glory. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> Whom have I in heaven but thee? and there is none upon earth that I desire beside thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> My flesh and my heart faileth: but God is the strength of my heart, and my portion for ever.^[**73:26** strength: Heb. rock] <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> For, lo, they that are far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that go a whoring from thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> But it is good for me to draw near to God: I have put my trust in the Lord GOD, that I may declare all thy works.











 

# 74 
Maschil of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O God, why hast thou cast us off for ever? why doth thine anger smoke against the sheep of thy pasture?^[**74:1** Maschil…: or, A Psalm for Asaph to give instruction] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Remember thy congregation, which thou hast purchased of old; the rod of thine inheritance, which thou hast redeemed; this mount Zion, wherein thou hast dwelt.^[**74:2** rod: or, tribe] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Lift up thy feet unto the perpetual desolations; even all that the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Thine enemies roar in the midst of thy congregations; they set up their ensigns for signs. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> A man was famous according as he had lifted up axes upon the thick trees. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> But now they break down the carved work thereof at once with axes and hammers. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> They have cast fire into thy sanctuary, they have defiled by casting down the dwelling place of thy name to the ground.^[**74:7** They have cast…: Heb. They have sent thy sanctuary unto the fire] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> They said in their hearts, Let us destroy them together: they have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land.^[**74:8** destroy: Heb. break] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> We see not our signs: there is no more any prophet: neither is there among us any that knoweth how long. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever? <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Why withdrawest thou thy hand, even thy right hand? pluck it out of thy bosom. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> For God is my King of old, working salvation in the midst of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thou didst divide the sea by thy strength: thou brakest the heads of the dragons in the waters.^[**74:13** divide: Heb. break]^[**74:13** dragons: or, whales] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Thou brakest the heads of leviathan in pieces, and gavest him to be meat to the people inhabiting the wilderness. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Thou didst cleave the fountain and the flood: thou driedst up mighty rivers.^[**74:15** mighty…: Heb. rivers of strength] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> The day is thine, the night also is thine: thou hast prepared the light and the sun. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Thou hast set all the borders of the earth: thou hast made summer and winter.^[**74:17** made: Heb. made them] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Remember this, that the enemy hath reproached, O LORD, and that the foolish people have blasphemed thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> O deliver not the soul of thy turtledove unto the multitude of the wicked: forget not the congregation of thy poor for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Have respect unto the covenant: for the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> O let not the oppressed return ashamed: let the poor and needy praise thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> Arise, O God, plead thine own cause: remember how the foolish man reproacheth thee daily. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Forget not the voice of thine enemies: the tumult of those that rise up against thee increaseth continually.^[**74:23** increaseth: Heb. ascendeth]








 

# 75 
To the chief Musician, Al-taschith, A Psalm or Song of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Unto thee, O God, do we give thanks, unto thee do we give thanks: for that thy name is near thy wondrous works declare.^[**75:1** Al-taschith: or, Destroy not]^[**75:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> When I shall receive the congregation I will judge uprightly.^[**75:2** receive…: or, take a set time] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The earth and all the inhabitants thereof are dissolved: I bear up the pillars of it. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> I said unto the fools, Deal not foolishly: and to the wicked, Lift not up the horn: <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Lift not up your horn on high: speak not with a stiff neck. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> For promotion cometh neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the south.^[**75:6** south: Heb. desert] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> But God is the judge: he putteth down one, and setteth up another. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> For in the hand of the LORD there is a cup, and the wine is red; it is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the same: but the dregs thereof, all the wicked of the earth shall wring them out, and drink them. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> But I will declare for ever; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> All the horns of the wicked also will I cut off; but the horns of the righteous shall be exalted.



 

# 76 
To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm or Song of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> In Judah is God known: his name is great in Israel.^[**76:1** chief…: or, overseer]^[**76:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> In Salem also is his tabernacle, and his dwelling place in Zion. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> There brake he the arrows of the bow, the shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Thou art more glorious and excellent than the mountains of prey. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The stouthearted are spoiled, they have slept their sleep: and none of the men of might have found their hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Thou, even thou, art to be feared: and who may stand in thy sight when once thou art angry? <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from heaven; the earth feared, and was still, <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> When God arose to judgment, to save all the meek of the earth. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Surely the wrath of man shall praise thee: the remainder of wrath shalt thou restrain. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Vow, and pay unto the LORD your God: let all that be round about him bring presents unto him that ought to be feared.^[**76:11** unto him…: Heb. to fear] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> He shall cut off the spirit of princes: he is terrible to the kings of the earth.


 

# 77 
To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I cried unto God with my voice, even unto God with my voice; and he gave ear unto me.^[**77:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord: my sore ran in the night, and ceased not: my soul refused to be comforted.^[**77:2** sore: Heb. hand] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> I remembered God, and was troubled: I complained, and my spirit was overwhelmed. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Thou holdest mine eyes waking: I am so troubled that I cannot speak. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I have considered the days of old, the years of ancient times. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I call to remembrance my song in the night: I commune with mine own heart: and my spirit made diligent search. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Will the Lord cast off for ever? and will he be favourable no more? <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Is his mercy clean gone for ever? doth his promise fail for evermore?^[**77:8** for evermore: Heb. to generation and generation?] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Hath God forgotten to be gracious? hath he in anger shut up his tender mercies? Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> And I said, This is my infirmity: but I will remember the years of the right hand of the most High. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> I will remember the works of the LORD: surely I will remember thy wonders of old. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> I will meditate also of all thy work, and talk of thy doings. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thy way, O God, is in the sanctuary: who is so great a God as our God? <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Thou art the God that doest wonders: thou hast declared thy strength among the people. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Thou hast with thine arm redeemed thy people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they were afraid: the depths also were troubled. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> The clouds poured out water: the skies sent out a sound: thine arrows also went abroad.^[**77:17** poured…: Heb. were poured forth with water] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> The voice of thy thunder was in the heaven: the lightnings lightened the world: the earth trembled and shook. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Thy way is in the sea, and thy path in the great waters, and thy footsteps are not known. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Thou leddest thy people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron.



 

# 78 
Maschil of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Give ear, O my people, to my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth.^[**78:1** Maschil…: or, A Psalm for Asaph to give instruction] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> I will open my mouth in a parable: I will utter dark sayings of old: <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told us. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> We will not hide them from their children, shewing to the generation to come the praises of the LORD, and his strength, and his wonderful works that he hath done. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a law in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children: <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> That the generation to come might know them, even the children which should be born; who should arise and declare them to their children: <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> That they might set their hope in God, and not forget the works of God, but keep his commandments: <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> And might not be as their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation; a generation that set not their heart aright, and whose spirit was not stedfast with God.^[**78:8** that…: Heb. that prepared not their heart] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> The children of Ephraim, being armed, and carrying bows, turned back in the day of battle.^[**78:9** carrying: Heb. throwing forth] <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> They kept not the covenant of God, and refused to walk in his law; <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> And forgat his works, and his wonders that he had shewed them. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Marvellous things did he in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> He divided the sea, and caused them to pass through; and he made the waters to stand as an heap. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> In the daytime also he led them with a cloud, and all the night with a light of fire. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> He clave the rocks in the wilderness, and gave them drink as out of the great depths. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> He brought streams also out of the rock, and caused waters to run down like rivers. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> And they sinned yet more against him by provoking the most High in the wilderness. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> And they tempted God in their heart by asking meat for their lust. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Yea, they spake against God; they said, Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?^[**78:19** furnish: Heb. order] <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Behold, he smote the rock, that the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed; can he give bread also? can he provide flesh for his people? <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Therefore the LORD heard this, and was wroth: so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and anger also came up against Israel; <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> Because they believed not in God, and trusted not in his salvation: <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Though he had commanded the clouds from above, and opened the doors of heaven, <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them of the corn of heaven. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> Man did eat angels’ food: he sent them meat to the full.^[**78:25** Man…: or, Every one did eat the bread of the mighty] <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven: and by his power he brought in the south wind.^[**78:26** to blow: Heb. to go] <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> He rained flesh also upon them as dust, and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea:^[**78:27** feathered…: Heb. fowl of wing] <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> And he let it fall in the midst of their camp, round about their habitations. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> So they did eat, and were well filled: for he gave them their own desire; <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> They were not estranged from their lust. But while their meat was yet in their mouths, <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> The wrath of God came upon them, and slew the fattest of them, and smote down the chosen men of Israel.^[**78:31** smote…: Heb. made to bow]^[**78:31** chosen…: or, young men] <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> For all this they sinned still, and believed not for his wondrous works. <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> Therefore their days did he consume in vanity, and their years in trouble. <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned and enquired early after God. <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> And they remembered that God was their rock, and the high God their redeemer. <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> Nevertheless they did flatter him with their mouth, and they lied unto him with their tongues. <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> For their heart was not right with him, neither were they stedfast in his covenant. <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> But he, being full of compassion, forgave their iniquity, and destroyed them not: yea, many a time turned he his anger away, and did not stir up all his wrath. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> For he remembered that they were but flesh; a wind that passeth away, and cometh not again. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, and grieve him in the desert!^[**78:40** provoke: or, rebel against] <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> Yea, they turned back and tempted God, and limited the Holy One of Israel. <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> They remembered not his hand, nor the day when he delivered them from the enemy.^[**78:42** from…: or, from affliction] <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> How he had wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Zoan:^[**78:43** wrought: Heb. set] <sup class='bibleverse'>44</sup> And had turned their rivers into blood; and their floods, that they could not drink. <sup class='bibleverse'>45</sup> He sent divers sorts of flies among them, which devoured them; and frogs, which destroyed them. <sup class='bibleverse'>46</sup> He gave also their increase unto the caterpiller, and their labour unto the locust. <sup class='bibleverse'>47</sup> He destroyed their vines with hail, and their sycomore trees with frost.^[**78:47** destroyed: Heb. killed]^[**78:47** frost: or, great hailstones] <sup class='bibleverse'>48</sup> He gave up their cattle also to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.^[**78:48** gave…: Heb. shut up]^[**78:48** hot…: or, lightnings] <sup class='bibleverse'>49</sup> He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, by sending evil angels among them. <sup class='bibleverse'>50</sup> He made a way to his anger; he spared not their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence;^[**78:50** He made…: Heb. He weighed a path]^[**78:50** life…: or, beasts to the murrain] <sup class='bibleverse'>51</sup> And smote all the firstborn in Egypt; the chief of their strength in the tabernacles of Ham: <sup class='bibleverse'>52</sup> But made his own people to go forth like sheep, and guided them in the wilderness like a flock. <sup class='bibleverse'>53</sup> And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.^[**78:53** overwhelmed: Heb. covered] <sup class='bibleverse'>54</sup> And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, even to this mountain, which his right hand had purchased. <sup class='bibleverse'>55</sup> He cast out the heathen also before them, and divided them an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents. <sup class='bibleverse'>56</sup> Yet they tempted and provoked the most high God, and kept not his testimonies: <sup class='bibleverse'>57</sup> But turned back, and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers: they were turned aside like a deceitful bow. <sup class='bibleverse'>58</sup> For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their graven images. <sup class='bibleverse'>59</sup> When God heard this, he was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel: <sup class='bibleverse'>60</sup> So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent which he placed among men; <sup class='bibleverse'>61</sup> And delivered his strength into captivity, and his glory into the enemy’s hand. <sup class='bibleverse'>62</sup> He gave his people over also unto the sword; and was wroth with his inheritance. <sup class='bibleverse'>63</sup> The fire consumed their young men; and their maidens were not given to marriage.^[**78:63** given…: Heb. praised] <sup class='bibleverse'>64</sup> Their priests fell by the sword; and their widows made no lamentation. <sup class='bibleverse'>65</sup> Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, and like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine. <sup class='bibleverse'>66</sup> And he smote his enemies in the hinder parts: he put them to a perpetual reproach. <sup class='bibleverse'>67</sup> Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, and chose not the tribe of Ephraim: <sup class='bibleverse'>68</sup> But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he loved. <sup class='bibleverse'>69</sup> And he built his sanctuary like high palaces, like the earth which he hath established for ever.^[**78:69** established: Heb. founded] <sup class='bibleverse'>70</sup> He chose David also his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds: <sup class='bibleverse'>71</sup> From following the ewes great with young he brought him to feed Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance.^[**78:71** following: Heb. after] <sup class='bibleverse'>72</sup> So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; and guided them by the skilfulness of his hands.





















 

# 79 
A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O God, the heathen are come into thine inheritance; thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid Jerusalem on heaps.^[**79:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The dead bodies of thy servants have they given to be meat unto the fowls of the heaven, the flesh of thy saints unto the beasts of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Their blood have they shed like water round about Jerusalem; and there was none to bury them. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> We are become a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and derision to them that are round about us. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> How long, LORD? wilt thou be angry for ever? shall thy jealousy burn like fire? <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Pour out thy wrath upon the heathen that have not known thee, and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> For they have devoured Jacob, and laid waste his dwelling place. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> O remember not against us former iniquities: let thy tender mercies speedily prevent us: for we are brought very low.^[**79:8** former…: or, the iniquities of them that were before us] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of thy name: and deliver us, and purge away our sins, for thy name’s sake. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is their God? let him be known among the heathen in our sight by the revenging of the blood of thy servants which is shed.^[**79:10** revenging: Heb. vengeance] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Let the sighing of the prisoner come before thee; according to the greatness of thy power preserve thou those that are appointed to die;^[**79:11** thy…: Heb. thine arm]^[**79:11** preserve…: Heb. reserve the children of death] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> And render unto our neighbours sevenfold into their bosom their reproach, wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> So we thy people and sheep of thy pasture will give thee thanks for ever: we will shew forth thy praise to all generations.^[**79:13** to all…: Heb. to generation and generation]





 

# 80 
To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim-eduth, A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest Joseph like a flock; thou that dwellest between the cherubims, shine forth.^[**80:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh stir up thy strength, and come and save us.^[**80:2** come…: Heb. come for salvation to us] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Turn us again, O God, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> O LORD God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy people?^[**80:4** be…: Heb. smoke] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Thou feedest them with the bread of tears; and givest them tears to drink in great measure. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Thou makest us a strife unto our neighbours: and our enemies laugh among themselves. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Turn us again, O God of hosts, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Thou hast brought a vine out of Egypt: thou hast cast out the heathen, and planted it. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Thou preparedst room before it, and didst cause it to take deep root, and it filled the land. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The hills were covered with the shadow of it, and the boughs thereof were like the goodly cedars.^[**80:10** goodly…: Heb. cedars of God] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> She sent out her boughs unto the sea, and her branches unto the river. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Why hast thou then broken down her hedges, so that all they which pass by the way do pluck her? <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> The boar out of the wood doth waste it, and the wild beast of the field doth devour it. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Return, we beseech thee, O God of hosts: look down from heaven, and behold, and visit this vine; <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> And the vineyard which thy right hand hath planted, and the branch that thou madest strong for thyself. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> It is burned with fire, it is cut down: they perish at the rebuke of thy countenance. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, upon the son of man whom thou madest strong for thyself. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> So will not we go back from thee: quicken us, and we will call upon thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Turn us again, O LORD God of hosts, cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.



 

# 81 
To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Sing aloud unto God our strength: make a joyful noise unto the God of Jacob.^[**81:1** of Asaph: or, for Asaph] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel, the pleasant harp with the psaltery. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Blow up the trumpet in the new moon, in the time appointed, on our solemn feast day. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For this was a statute for Israel, and a law of the God of Jacob. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> This he ordained in Joseph for a testimony, when he went out through the land of Egypt: where I heard a language that I understood not.^[**81:5** through: or, against] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I removed his shoulder from the burden: his hands were delivered from the pots.^[**81:6** were…: Heb. passed away] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: I proved thee at the waters of Meribah. Selah.^[**81:7** Meribah: or, Strife] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Hear, O my people, and I will testify unto thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken unto me; <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> There shall no strange god be in thee; neither shalt thou worship any strange god. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> I am the LORD thy God, which brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> But my people would not hearken to my voice; and Israel would none of me. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> So I gave them up unto their own hearts’ lust: and they walked in their own counsels.^[**81:12** unto…: or, to the hardness of their hearts, or, imagination] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Oh that my people had hearkened unto me, and Israel had walked in my ways! <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> I should soon have subdued their enemies, and turned my hand against their adversaries. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> The haters of the LORD should have submitted themselves unto him: but their time should have endured for ever.^[**81:15** submitted…: or, yielded feigned obedience: Heb. lied] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> He should have fed them also with the finest of the wheat: and with honey out of the rock should I have satisfied thee.^[**81:16** finest…: Heb. fat of wheat]






 

# 82 
A Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> God standeth in the congregation of the mighty; he judgeth among the gods.^[**82:1** of Asaph: or, for Asaph] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> How long will ye judge unjustly, and accept the persons of the wicked? Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Defend the poor and fatherless: do justice to the afflicted and needy.^[**82:3** Defend: Heb. Judge] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Deliver the poor and needy: rid them out of the hand of the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They know not, neither will they understand; they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth are out of course.^[**82:5** out…: Heb. moved] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I have said, Ye are gods; and all of you are children of the most High. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> But ye shall die like men, and fall like one of the princes. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Arise, O God, judge the earth: for thou shalt inherit all nations.


 

# 83 
A Song or Psalm of Asaph. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Keep not thou silence, O God: hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God.^[**83:1** of Asaph: or, for Asaph] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> For, lo, thine enemies make a tumult: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> They have taken crafty counsel against thy people, and consulted against thy hidden ones. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> They have said, Come, and let us cut them off from being a nation; that the name of Israel may be no more in remembrance. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For they have consulted together with one consent: they are confederate against thee:^[**83:5** consent: Heb. heart] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The tabernacles of Edom, and the Ishmaelites; of Moab, and the Hagarenes; <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; the Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre; <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Assur also is joined with them: they have holpen the children of Lot. Selah.^[**83:8** holpen: Heb. been an arm to] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Do unto them as unto the Midianites; as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the brook of Kison: <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Which perished at Endor: they became as dung for the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Make their nobles like Oreb, and like Zeeb: yea, all their princes as Zebah, and as Zalmunna: <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Who said, Let us take to ourselves the houses of God in possession. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> O my God, make them like a wheel; as the stubble before the wind. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> As the fire burneth a wood, and as the flame setteth the mountains on fire; <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> So persecute them with thy tempest, and make them afraid with thy storm. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Fill their faces with shame; that they may seek thy name, O LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Let them be confounded and troubled for ever; yea, let them be put to shame, and perish: <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> That men may know that thou, whose name alone is JEHOVAH, art the most high over all the earth.


 

# 84 
To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> How amiable are thy tabernacles, O LORD of hosts!^[**84:1** for the sons: or, of the sons] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> My soul longeth, yea, even fainteth for the courts of the LORD: my heart and my flesh crieth out for the living God. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Yea, the sparrow hath found an house, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may lay her young, even thine altars, O LORD of hosts, my King, and my God. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Blessed are they that dwell in thy house: they will be still praising thee. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Blessed is the man whose strength is in thee; in whose heart are the ways of them. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Who passing through the valley of Baca make it a well; the rain also filleth the pools.^[**84:6** Baca…: or, mulberry trees make him a well, etc]^[**84:6** filleth: Heb. covereth] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> They go from strength to strength, every one of them in Zion appeareth before God.^[**84:7** strength to…: or, company to company] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> O LORD God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Behold, O God our shield, and look upon the face of thine anointed. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> For a day in thy courts is better than a thousand. I had rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.^[**84:10** I had…: Heb. I would choose rather to sit at the threshold] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> For the LORD God is a sun and shield: the LORD will give grace and glory: no good thing will he withhold from them that walk uprightly. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> O LORD of hosts, blessed is the man that trusteth in thee.




 

# 85 
To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> LORD, thou hast been favourable unto thy land: thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob.^[**85:1** for the sons: or, of the sons]^[**85:1** favourable: or, well pleased] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people, thou hast covered all their sin. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Thou hast taken away all thy wrath: thou hast turned thyself from the fierceness of thine anger.^[**85:3** thyself…: or, thine anger from waxing hot] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Turn us, O God of our salvation, and cause thine anger toward us to cease. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? wilt thou draw out thine anger to all generations? <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Wilt thou not revive us again: that thy people may rejoice in thee? <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Shew us thy mercy, O LORD, and grant us thy salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> I will hear what God the LORD will speak: for he will speak peace unto his people, and to his saints: but let them not turn again to folly. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Surely his salvation is nigh them that fear him; that glory may dwell in our land. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Mercy and truth are met together; righteousness and peace have kissed each other. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Truth shall spring out of the earth; and righteousness shall look down from heaven. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Yea, the LORD shall give that which is good; and our land shall yield her increase. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Righteousness shall go before him; and shall set us in the way of his steps.


 

# 86 
A Prayer of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Bow down thine ear, O LORD, hear me: for I am poor and needy.^[**86:1** A Prayer…: or, A Prayer, being a Psalm of David] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Preserve my soul; for I am holy: O thou my God, save thy servant that trusteth in thee.^[**86:2** holy: or, one whom thou favourest] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Be merciful unto me, O Lord: for I cry unto thee daily.^[**86:3** daily: or, all the day] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Rejoice the soul of thy servant: for unto thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For thou, Lord, art good, and ready to forgive; and plenteous in mercy unto all them that call upon thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Give ear, O LORD, unto my prayer; and attend to the voice of my supplications. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> In the day of my trouble I will call upon thee: for thou wilt answer me. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Among the gods there is none like unto thee, O Lord; neither are there any works like unto thy works. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship before thee, O Lord; and shall glorify thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> For thou art great, and doest wondrous things: thou art God alone. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Teach me thy way, O LORD; I will walk in thy truth: unite my heart to fear thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart: and I will glorify thy name for evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> For great is thy mercy toward me: and thou hast delivered my soul from the lowest hell.^[**86:13** hell: or, grave] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> O God, the proud are risen against me, and the assemblies of violent men have sought after my soul; and have not set thee before them.^[**86:14** violent: Heb. terrible] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> But thou, O Lord, art a God full of compassion, and gracious, longsuffering, and plenteous in mercy and truth. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> O turn unto me, and have mercy upon me; give thy strength unto thy servant, and save the son of thine handmaid. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Shew me a token for good; that they which hate me may see it, and be ashamed: because thou, LORD, hast holpen me, and comforted me.




 

# 87 
A Psalm or Song for the sons of Korah. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> His foundation is in the holy mountains.^[**87:1** for the sons: or, of the sons] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The LORD loveth the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Glorious things are spoken of thee, O city of God. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon to them that know me: behold Philistia, and Tyre, with Ethiopia; this man was born there. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> And of Zion it shall be said, This and that man was born in her: and the highest himself shall establish her. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The LORD shall count, when he writeth up the people, that this man was born there. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> As well the singers as the players on instruments shall be there: all my springs are in thee.
 

# 88 
A Song or Psalm for the sons of Korah, to the chief Musician upon Mahalath Leannoth, Maschil of Heman the Ezrahite. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O LORD God of my salvation, I have cried day and night before thee:^[**88:1** for the sons: or, of the sons]^[**88:1** Maschil…: or, A Psalm of Heman the Ezrahite, giving instruction] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let my prayer come before thee: incline thine ear unto my cry; <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For my soul is full of troubles: and my life draweth nigh unto the grave. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> I am counted with them that go down into the pit: I am as a man that hath no strength: <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Free among the dead, like the slain that lie in the grave, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cut off from thy hand.^[**88:5** from: or, by] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, in darkness, in the deeps. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Thy wrath lieth hard upon me, and thou hast afflicted me with all thy waves. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Thou hast put away mine acquaintance far from me; thou hast made me an abomination unto them: I am shut up, and I cannot come forth. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Mine eye mourneth by reason of affliction: LORD, I have called daily upon thee, I have stretched out my hands unto thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? shall the dead arise and praise thee? Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Shall thy lovingkindness be declared in the grave? or thy faithfulness in destruction? <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? and thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness? <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> But unto thee have I cried, O LORD; and in the morning shall my prayer prevent thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> LORD, why castest thou off my soul? why hidest thou thy face from me? <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth up: while I suffer thy terrors I am distracted. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Thy fierce wrath goeth over me; thy terrors have cut me off. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> They came round about me daily like water; they compassed me about together.^[**88:17** daily: or, all the day] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Lover and friend hast thou put far from me, and mine acquaintance into darkness.



 

# 89 
Maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I will sing of the mercies of the LORD for ever: with my mouth will I make known thy faithfulness to all generations.^[**89:1** Maschil…: or, A Psalm for Ethan the Ezrahite, to give instruction]^[**89:1** to all…: Heb. to generation and generation] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> For I have said, Mercy shall be built up for ever: thy faithfulness shalt thou establish in the very heavens. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> I have made a covenant with my chosen, I have sworn unto David my servant, <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Thy seed will I establish for ever, and build up thy throne to all generations. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> And the heavens shall praise thy wonders, O LORD: thy faithfulness also in the congregation of the saints. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> For who in the heaven can be compared unto the LORD? who among the sons of the mighty can be likened unto the LORD? <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> God is greatly to be feared in the assembly of the saints, and to be had in reverence of all them that are about him. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> O LORD God of hosts, who is a strong LORD like unto thee? or to thy faithfulness round about thee? <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Thou rulest the raging of the sea: when the waves thereof arise, thou stillest them. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Thou hast broken Rahab in pieces, as one that is slain; thou hast scattered thine enemies with thy strong arm.^[**89:10** Rahab: or, Egypt]^[**89:10** thy…: Heb. the arm of thy strength] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> The heavens are thine, the earth also is thine: as for the world and the fulness thereof, thou hast founded them.^[**89:11** the fulness…: or, all it containeth] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> The north and the south thou hast created them: Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thou hast a mighty arm: strong is thy hand, and high is thy right hand.^[**89:13** a…: Heb. an arm with might] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Justice and judgment are the habitation of thy throne: mercy and truth shall go before thy face.^[**89:14** habitation: or, establishment] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Blessed is the people that know the joyful sound: they shall walk, O LORD, in the light of thy countenance. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> In thy name shall they rejoice all the day: and in thy righteousness shall they be exalted. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> For thou art the glory of their strength: and in thy favour our horn shall be exalted. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> For the LORD is our defence; and the Holy One of Israel is our king.^[**89:18** the LORD…: or, our shield is of the LORD, and our king is of the Holy One of Israel] <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Then thou spakest in vision to thy holy one, and saidst, I have laid help upon one that is mighty; I have exalted one chosen out of the people. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> I have found David my servant; with my holy oil have I anointed him: <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> With whom my hand shall be established: mine arm also shall strengthen him. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> The enemy shall not exact upon him; nor the son of wickedness afflict him. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> And I will beat down his foes before his face, and plague them that hate him. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> But my faithfulness and my mercy shall be with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> I will set his hand also in the sea, and his right hand in the rivers. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> He shall cry unto me, Thou art my father, my God, and the rock of my salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> Also I will make him my firstborn, higher than the kings of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> My mercy will I keep for him for evermore, and my covenant shall stand fast with him. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> His seed also will I make to endure for ever, and his throne as the days of heaven. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> If his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments; <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> If they break my statutes, and keep not my commandments;^[**89:31** break: Heb. profane] <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> Then will I visit their transgression with the rod, and their iniquity with stripes. <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> Nevertheless my lovingkindness will I not utterly take from him, nor suffer my faithfulness to fail.^[**89:33** will…: Heb. I will not make void from him]^[**89:33** to fail: Heb. to lie] <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> My covenant will I not break, nor alter the thing that is gone out of my lips. <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> Once have I sworn by my holiness that I will not lie unto David.^[**89:35** that…: Heb. if I lie] <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> His seed shall endure for ever, and his throne as the sun before me. <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> It shall be established for ever as the moon, and as a faithful witness in heaven. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> But thou hast cast off and abhorred, thou hast been wroth with thine anointed. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his crown by casting it to the ground. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> Thou hast broken down all his hedges; thou hast brought his strong holds to ruin. <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> All that pass by the way spoil him: he is a reproach to his neighbours. <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> Thou hast set up the right hand of his adversaries; thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice. <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> Thou hast also turned the edge of his sword, and hast not made him to stand in the battle. <sup class='bibleverse'>44</sup> Thou hast made his glory to cease, and cast his throne down to the ground.^[**89:44** glory: Heb. brightness] <sup class='bibleverse'>45</sup> The days of his youth hast thou shortened: thou hast covered him with shame. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>46</sup> How long, LORD? wilt thou hide thyself for ever? shall thy wrath burn like fire? <sup class='bibleverse'>47</sup> Remember how short my time is: wherefore hast thou made all men in vain? <sup class='bibleverse'>48</sup> What man is he that liveth, and shall not see death? shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>49</sup> Lord, where are thy former lovingkindnesses, which thou swarest unto David in thy truth? <sup class='bibleverse'>50</sup> Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants; how I do bear in my bosom the reproach of all the mighty people; <sup class='bibleverse'>51</sup> Wherewith thine enemies have reproached, O LORD; wherewith they have reproached the footsteps of thine anointed. <sup class='bibleverse'>52</sup> Blessed be the LORD for evermore. Amen, and Amen.












 

# 90 
A Prayer of Moses the man of God. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Lord, thou hast been our dwelling place in all generations.^[**90:1** A Prayer…: or, A Prayer, being a Psalm of Moses]^[**90:1** in…: Heb. in generation and generation] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Before the mountains were brought forth, or ever thou hadst formed the earth and the world, even from everlasting to everlasting, thou art God. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Thou turnest man to destruction; and sayest, Return, ye children of men. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For a thousand years in thy sight are but as yesterday when it is past, and as a watch in the night.^[**90:4** when…: or, when he hath passed them] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Thou carriest them away as with a flood; they are as a sleep: in the morning they are like grass which groweth up.^[**90:5** groweth…: or, is changed] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> In the morning it flourisheth, and groweth up; in the evening it is cut down, and withereth. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> For we are consumed by thine anger, and by thy wrath are we troubled. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, our secret sins in the light of thy countenance. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> For all our days are passed away in thy wrath: we spend our years as a tale that is told.^[**90:9** passed…: Heb. turned away]^[**90:9** as a…: or, as a meditation] <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The days of our years are threescore years and ten; and if by reason of strength they be fourscore years, yet is their strength labour and sorrow; for it is soon cut off, and we fly away.^[**90:10** The days…: Heb. As for the days of our years, in them are seventy years] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Who knoweth the power of thine anger? even according to thy fear, so is thy wrath. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> So teach us to number our days, that we may apply our hearts unto wisdom.^[**90:12** apply: Heb. cause to come] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Return, O LORD, how long? and let it repent thee concerning thy servants. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> O satisfy us early with thy mercy; that we may rejoice and be glad all our days. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Make us glad according to the days wherein thou hast afflicted us, and the years wherein we have seen evil. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Let thy work appear unto thy servants, and thy glory unto their children. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> And let the beauty of the LORD our God be upon us: and establish thou the work of our hands upon us; yea, the work of our hands establish thou it.







 

# 91 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> He that dwelleth in the secret place of the most High shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty.^[**91:1** abide: Heb. lodge] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> I will say of the LORD, He is my refuge and my fortress: my God; in him will I trust. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler, and from the noisome pestilence. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings shalt thou trust: his truth shall be thy shield and buckler. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Thou shalt not be afraid for the terror by night; nor for the arrow that flieth by day; <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Nor for the pestilence that walketh in darkness; nor for the destruction that wasteth at noonday. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand; but it shall not come nigh thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Only with thine eyes shalt thou behold and see the reward of the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Because thou hast made the LORD, which is my refuge, even the most High, thy habitation; <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> There shall no evil befall thee, neither shall any plague come nigh thy dwelling. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> For he shall give his angels charge over thee, to keep thee in all thy ways. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> They shall bear thee up in their hands, lest thou dash thy foot against a stone. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thou shalt tread upon the lion and adder: the young lion and the dragon shalt thou trample under feet.^[**91:13** adder: or, asp] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Because he hath set his love upon me, therefore will I deliver him: I will set him on high, because he hath known my name. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> He shall call upon me, and I will answer him: I will be with him in trouble; I will deliver him, and honour him. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> With long life will I satisfy him, and shew him my salvation.^[**91:16** long…: Heb. length of days]


 

# 92 
A Psalm or Song for the sabbath day. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> It is a good thing to give thanks unto the LORD, and to sing praises unto thy name, O most High: <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> To shew forth thy lovingkindness in the morning, and thy faithfulness every night,^[**92:2** every…: Heb. in the nights] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Upon an instrument of ten strings, and upon the psaltery; upon the harp with a solemn sound.^[**92:3** the harp…: or, the solemn sound with the harp]^[**92:3** a solemn…: Heb. Higgaion] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For thou, LORD, hast made me glad through thy work: I will triumph in the works of thy hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> O LORD, how great are thy works! and thy thoughts are very deep. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> A brutish man knoweth not; neither doth a fool understand this. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> When the wicked spring as the grass, and when all the workers of iniquity do flourish; it is that they shall be destroyed for ever: <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> But thou, LORD, art most high for evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> For, lo, thine enemies, O LORD, for, lo, thine enemies shall perish; all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> But my horn shalt thou exalt like the horn of an unicorn: I shall be anointed with fresh oil. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Mine eye also shall see my desire on mine enemies, and mine ears shall hear my desire of the wicked that rise up against me. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree: he shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Those that be planted in the house of the LORD shall flourish in the courts of our God. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> They shall still bring forth fruit in old age; they shall be fat and flourishing;^[**92:14** flourishing: Heb. green] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> To shew that the LORD is upright: he is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in him.



 

# 93 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> The LORD reigneth, he is clothed with majesty; the LORD is clothed with strength, wherewith he hath girded himself: the world also is stablished, that it cannot be moved. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Thy throne is established of old: thou art from everlasting.^[**93:2** of old: Heb. from then] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The floods have lifted up, O LORD, the floods have lifted up their voice; the floods lift up their waves. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The LORD on high is mightier than the noise of many waters, yea, than the mighty waves of the sea. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Thy testimonies are very sure: holiness becometh thine house, O LORD, for ever.^[**93:5** for ever: Heb. to length of days]

 

# 94 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O LORD God, to whom vengeance belongeth; O God, to whom vengeance belongeth, shew thyself.^[**94:1** God…: Heb. God of revenges]^[**94:1** shew…: Heb. shine forth] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth: render a reward to the proud. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> LORD, how long shall the wicked, how long shall the wicked triumph? <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> How long shall they utter and speak hard things? and all the workers of iniquity boast themselves? <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They break in pieces thy people, O LORD, and afflict thine heritage. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> They slay the widow and the stranger, and murder the fatherless. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Yet they say, The LORD shall not see, neither shall the God of Jacob regard it. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Understand, ye brutish among the people: and ye fools, when will ye be wise? <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? he that formed the eye, shall he not see? <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> He that chastiseth the heathen, shall not he correct? he that teacheth man knowledge, shall not he know? <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> The LORD knoweth the thoughts of man, that they are vanity. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Blessed is the man whom thou chastenest, O LORD, and teachest him out of thy law; <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> That thou mayest give him rest from the days of adversity, until the pit be digged for the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> For the LORD will not cast off his people, neither will he forsake his inheritance. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> But judgment shall return unto righteousness: and all the upright in heart shall follow it.^[**94:15** shall follow…: Heb. shall be after it] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Who will rise up for me against the evildoers? or who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity? <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Unless the LORD had been my help, my soul had almost dwelt in silence.^[**94:17** almost: or, quickly] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> When I said, My foot slippeth; thy mercy, O LORD, held me up. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> In the multitude of my thoughts within me thy comforts delight my soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with thee, which frameth mischief by a law? <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> They gather themselves together against the soul of the righteous, and condemn the innocent blood. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> But the LORD is my defence; and my God is the rock of my refuge. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> And he shall bring upon them their own iniquity, and shall cut them off in their own wickedness; yea, the LORD our God shall cut them off.



 

# 95 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O come, let us sing unto the LORD: let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving, and make a joyful noise unto him with psalms.^[**95:2** come…: Heb. prevent his face] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For the LORD is a great God, and a great King above all gods. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> In his hand are the deep places of the earth: the strength of the hills is his also.^[**95:4** In…: Heb. In whose]^[**95:4** the strength…: or, the heights of the hills are his] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The sea is his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry land.^[**95:5** The sea…: Heb. Whose the sea is] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> O come, let us worship and bow down: let us kneel before the LORD our maker. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> For he is our God; and we are the people of his pasture, and the sheep of his hand. To day if ye will hear his voice, <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Harden not your heart, as in the provocation, and as in the day of temptation in the wilderness:^[**95:8** provocation: Heb. contention] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> When your fathers tempted me, proved me, and saw my work. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Forty years long was I grieved with this generation, and said, It is a people that do err in their heart, and they have not known my ways: <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Unto whom I sware in my wrath that they should not enter into my rest.^[**95:11** that…: Heb. if they enter into my rest]





 

# 96 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O sing unto the LORD a new song: sing unto the LORD, all the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Sing unto the LORD, bless his name; shew forth his salvation from day to day. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Declare his glory among the heathen, his wonders among all people. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For the LORD is great, and greatly to be praised: he is to be feared above all gods. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For all the gods of the nations are idols: but the LORD made the heavens. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Honour and majesty are before him: strength and beauty are in his sanctuary. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Give unto the LORD, O ye kindreds of the people, give unto the LORD glory and strength. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Give unto the LORD the glory due unto his name: bring an offering, and come into his courts.^[**96:8** due…: Heb. of his name] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> O worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness: fear before him, all the earth.^[**96:9** in the…: or, in the glorious sanctuary] <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Say among the heathen that the LORD reigneth: the world also shall be established that it shall not be moved: he shall judge the people righteously. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad; let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof.^[**96:11** the fulness…: or, all it containeth] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Let the field be joyful, and all that is therein: then shall all the trees of the wood rejoice <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Before the LORD: for he cometh, for he cometh to judge the earth: he shall judge the world with righteousness, and the people with his truth.


 

# 97 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> The LORD reigneth; let the earth rejoice; let the multitude of isles be glad thereof.^[**97:1** multitude…: Heb. many, or, great isles] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Clouds and darkness are round about him: righteousness and judgment are the habitation of his throne.^[**97:2** habitation: or, establishment] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> A fire goeth before him, and burneth up his enemies round about. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> His lightnings enlightened the world: the earth saw, and trembled. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The hills melted like wax at the presence of the LORD, at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The heavens declare his righteousness, and all the people see his glory. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Confounded be all they that serve graven images, that boast themselves of idols: worship him, all ye gods. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Zion heard, and was glad; and the daughters of Judah rejoiced because of thy judgments, O LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> For thou, LORD, art high above all the earth: thou art exalted far above all gods. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Ye that love the LORD, hate evil: he preserveth the souls of his saints; he delivereth them out of the hand of the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Light is sown for the righteous, and gladness for the upright in heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Rejoice in the LORD, ye righteous; and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.^[**97:12** at…: or, to the memorial]


 

# 98 
A Psalm. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O sing unto the LORD a new song; for he hath done marvellous things: his right hand, and his holy arm, hath gotten him the victory. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The LORD hath made known his salvation: his righteousness hath he openly shewed in the sight of the heathen.^[**98:2** openly…: or, revealed] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> He hath remembered his mercy and his truth toward the house of Israel: all the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Make a joyful noise unto the LORD, all the earth: make a loud noise, and rejoice, and sing praise. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Sing unto the LORD with the harp; with the harp, and the voice of a psalm. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> With trumpets and sound of cornet make a joyful noise before the LORD, the King. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.^[**98:7** the fulness…: or, all it containeth] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Let the floods clap their hands: let the hills be joyful together <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Before the LORD; for he cometh to judge the earth: with righteousness shall he judge the world, and the people with equity.

 

# 99 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> The LORD reigneth; let the people tremble: he sitteth between the cherubims; let the earth be moved.^[**99:1** be moved: Heb. stagger] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The LORD is great in Zion; and he is high above all the people. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Let them praise thy great and terrible name; for it is holy. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The king’s strength also loveth judgment; thou dost establish equity, thou executest judgment and righteousness in Jacob. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Exalt ye the LORD our God, and worship at his footstool; for he is holy.^[**99:5** he is…: or, it is holy] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among them that call upon his name; they called upon the LORD, and he answered them. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He spake unto them in the cloudy pillar: they kept his testimonies, and the ordinance that he gave them. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Thou answeredst them, O LORD our God: thou wast a God that forgavest them, though thou tookest vengeance of their inventions. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Exalt the LORD our God, and worship at his holy hill; for the LORD our God is holy.

 

# 100 
A Psalm of praise. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Make a joyful noise unto the LORD, all ye lands.^[**100:1** praise: or, thanksgiving]^[**100:1** all…: Heb. all the earth] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Serve the LORD with gladness: come before his presence with singing. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Know ye that the LORD he is God: it is he that hath made us, and not we ourselves; we are his people, and the sheep of his pasture.^[**100:3** and not…: or, and his we are] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Enter into his gates with thanksgiving, and into his courts with praise: be thankful unto him, and bless his name. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For the LORD is good; his mercy is everlasting; and his truth endureth to all generations.^[**100:5** to all…: Heb. to generation and generation]



 

# 101 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I will sing of mercy and judgment: unto thee, O LORD, will I sing. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. O when wilt thou come unto me? I will walk within my house with a perfect heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> I will set no wicked thing before mine eyes: I hate the work of them that turn aside; it shall not cleave to me.^[**101:3** wicked…: Heb. thing of Belial] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> A froward heart shall depart from me: I will not know a wicked person. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Whoso privily slandereth his neighbour, him will I cut off: him that hath an high look and a proud heart will not I suffer. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Mine eyes shall be upon the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me: he that walketh in a perfect way, he shall serve me.^[**101:6** in a…: or, perfect in the way] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He that worketh deceit shall not dwell within my house: he that telleth lies shall not tarry in my sight.^[**101:7** shall not tarry: Heb. shall not be established] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> I will early destroy all the wicked of the land; that I may cut off all wicked doers from the city of the LORD.


 

# 102 
A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed, and poureth out his complaint before the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Hear my prayer, O LORD, and let my cry come unto thee.^[**102:1** of: or, for] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Hide not thy face from me in the day when I am in trouble; incline thine ear unto me: in the day when I call answer me speedily. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are burned as an hearth.^[**102:3** like…: or, (as some read) into smoke] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> My heart is smitten, and withered like grass; so that I forget to eat my bread. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> By reason of the voice of my groaning my bones cleave to my skin.^[**102:5** skin: or, flesh] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I am like a pelican of the wilderness: I am like an owl of the desert. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> I watch, and am as a sparrow alone upon the house top. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Mine enemies reproach me all the day; and they that are mad against me are sworn against me. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping, <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Because of thine indignation and thy wrath: for thou hast lifted me up, and cast me down. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> My days are like a shadow that declineth; and I am withered like grass. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> But thou, O LORD, shalt endure for ever; and thy remembrance unto all generations. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thou shalt arise, and have mercy upon Zion: for the time to favour her, yea, the set time, is come. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, and favour the dust thereof. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> So the heathen shall fear the name of the LORD, and all the kings of the earth thy glory. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> When the LORD shall build up Zion, he shall appear in his glory. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> He will regard the prayer of the destitute, and not despise their prayer. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> This shall be written for the generation to come: and the people which shall be created shall praise the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> For he hath looked down from the height of his sanctuary; from heaven did the LORD behold the earth; <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> To hear the groaning of the prisoner; to loose those that are appointed to death;^[**102:20** those…: Heb. the children of death] <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> To declare the name of the LORD in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem; <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> When the people are gathered together, and the kingdoms, to serve the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> He weakened my strength in the way; he shortened my days.^[**102:23** weakened: Heb. afflicted] <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> I said, O my God, take me not away in the midst of my days: thy years are throughout all generations. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> Of old hast thou laid the foundation of the earth: and the heavens are the work of thy hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> They shall perish, but thou shalt endure: yea, all of them shall wax old like a garment; as a vesture shalt thou change them, and they shall be changed:^[**102:26** endure: Heb. stand] <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> But thou art the same, and thy years shall have no end. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> The children of thy servants shall continue, and their seed shall be established before thee.





 

# 103 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Bless the LORD, O my soul: and all that is within me, bless his holy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Bless the LORD, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits: <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Who forgiveth all thine iniquities; who healeth all thy diseases; <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; who crowneth thee with lovingkindness and tender mercies; <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Who satisfieth thy mouth with good things; so that thy youth is renewed like the eagle’s. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The LORD executeth righteousness and judgment for all that are oppressed. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He made known his ways unto Moses, his acts unto the children of Israel. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> The LORD is merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and plenteous in mercy.^[**103:8** plenteous…: Heb. great in mercy] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He will not always chide: neither will he keep his anger for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> He hath not dealt with us after our sins; nor rewarded us according to our iniquities. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> For as the heaven is high above the earth, so great is his mercy toward them that fear him.^[**103:11** as…: Heb. according to the height of the heaven] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he removed our transgressions from us. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Like as a father pitieth his children, so the LORD pitieth them that fear him. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> For he knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we are dust. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> As for man, his days are as grass: as a flower of the field, so he flourisheth. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; and the place thereof shall know it no more.^[**103:16** it is…: Heb. it is not] <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> But the mercy of the LORD is from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, and his righteousness unto children’s children; <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> To such as keep his covenant, and to those that remember his commandments to do them. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> The LORD hath prepared his throne in the heavens; and his kingdom ruleth over all. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Bless the LORD, ye his angels, that excel in strength, that do his commandments, hearkening unto the voice of his word.^[**103:20** that excel…: Heb. mighty in strength] <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Bless ye the LORD, all ye his hosts; ye ministers of his, that do his pleasure. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> Bless the LORD, all his works in all places of his dominion: bless the LORD, O my soul.



 

# 104
