<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Bless the LORD, O my soul. O LORD my God, thou art very great; thou art clothed with honour and majesty. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Who coverest thyself with light as with a garment: who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain: <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: who maketh the clouds his chariot: who walketh upon the wings of the wind: <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flaming fire: <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Who laid the foundations of the earth, that it should not be removed for ever.^[**104:5** Who…: Heb. He hath founded the earth upon her bases] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Thou coveredst it with the deep as with a garment: the waters stood above the mountains. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> At thy rebuke they fled; at the voice of thy thunder they hasted away. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys unto the place which thou hast founded for them.^[**104:8** They go up…: or, The mountains ascend, the valleys descend] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; that they turn not again to cover the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> He sendeth the springs into the valleys, which run among the hills.^[**104:10** He: Heb. Who]^[**104:10** run: Heb. walk] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> They give drink to every beast of the field: the wild asses quench their thirst.^[**104:11** quench: Heb. break] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, which sing among the branches.^[**104:12** sing: Heb. give a voice] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> He watereth the hills from his chambers: the earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for the service of man: that he may bring forth food out of the earth; <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> And wine that maketh glad the heart of man, and oil to make his face to shine, and bread which strengtheneth man’s heart.^[**104:15** oil…: Heb. to make his face shine with oil, or, more than oil] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> The trees of the LORD are full of sap; the cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted; <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Where the birds make their nests: as for the stork, the fir trees are her house. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> The high hills are a refuge for the wild goats; and the rocks for the conies. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> He appointed the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Thou makest darkness, and it is night: wherein all the beasts of the forest do creep forth.^[**104:20** beasts…: Heb. beasts thereof do trample on the forest] <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their meat from God. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> The sun ariseth, they gather themselves together, and lay them down in their dens. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Man goeth forth unto his work and to his labour until the evening. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> O LORD, how manifold are thy works! in wisdom hast thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> So is this great and wide sea, wherein are things creeping innumerable, both small and great beasts. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> There go the ships: there is that leviathan, whom thou hast made to play therein.^[**104:26** made: Heb. formed] <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> These wait all upon thee; that thou mayest give them their meat in due season. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> That thou givest them they gather: thou openest thine hand, they are filled with good. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: and thou renewest the face of the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> The glory of the LORD shall endure for ever: the LORD shall rejoice in his works.^[**104:31** endure: Heb. be] <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth: he toucheth the hills, and they smoke. <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> I will sing unto the LORD as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being. <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> Let the sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the LORD, O my soul. Praise ye the LORD.









 

# 105 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O give thanks unto the LORD; call upon his name: make known his deeds among the people. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him: talk ye of all his wondrous works. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Seek the LORD, and his strength: seek his face evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Remember his marvellous works that he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth; <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> O ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye children of Jacob his chosen. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He is the LORD our God: his judgments are in all the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> He hath remembered his covenant for ever, the word which he commanded to a thousand generations. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Which covenant he made with Abraham, and his oath unto Isaac; <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> And confirmed the same unto Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting covenant: <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Saying, Unto thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance:^[**105:11** lot: Heb. cord] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> When they were but a few men in number; yea, very few, and strangers in it. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> When they went from one nation to another, from one kingdom to another people; <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He suffered no man to do them wrong: yea, he reproved kings for their sakes; <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Saying, Touch not mine anointed, and do my prophets no harm. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: he brake the whole staff of bread. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> He sent a man before them, even Joseph, who was sold for a servant: <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Whose feet they hurt with fetters: he was laid in iron:^[**105:18** he…: Heb. his soul came into iron] <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Until the time that his word came: the word of the LORD tried him. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> The king sent and loosed him; even the ruler of the people, and let him go free. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all his substance:^[**105:21** substance: Heb. possession] <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> To bind his princes at his pleasure; and teach his senators wisdom. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Israel also came into Egypt; and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> And he increased his people greatly; and made them stronger than their enemies. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal subtilly with his servants. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> He sent Moses his servant; and Aaron whom he had chosen. <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> They shewed his signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.^[**105:27** his…: Heb. words of his signs] <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not against his word. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> He turned their waters into blood, and slew their fish. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, in the chambers of their kings. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> He spake, and there came divers sorts of flies, and lice in all their coasts. <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> He gave them hail for rain, and flaming fire in their land.^[**105:32** them…: Heb. their rain hail] <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> He smote their vines also and their fig trees; and brake the trees of their coasts. <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> He spake, and the locusts came, and caterpillers, and that without number, <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> And did eat up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground. <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> He smote also all the firstborn in their land, the chief of all their strength. <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> He brought them forth also with silver and gold: and there was not one feeble person among their tribes. <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them fell upon them. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> He spread a cloud for a covering; and fire to give light in the night. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> The people asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of heaven. <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; they ran in the dry places like a river. <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> For he remembered his holy promise, and Abraham his servant. <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> And he brought forth his people with joy, and his chosen with gladness:^[**105:43** gladness: Heb. singing] <sup class='bibleverse'>44</sup> And gave them the lands of the heathen: and they inherited the labour of the people; <sup class='bibleverse'>45</sup> That they might observe his statutes, and keep his laws. Praise ye the LORD.^[**105:45** Praise…: Heb. Hallelujah]






 

# 106 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.^[**106:1** Praise…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD? who can shew forth all his praise? <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Blessed are they that keep judgment, and he that doeth righteousness at all times. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Remember me, O LORD, with the favour that thou bearest unto thy people: O visit me with thy salvation; <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> That I may see the good of thy chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of thy nation, that I may glory with thine inheritance. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; but provoked him at the sea, even at the Red sea. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Nevertheless he saved them for his name’s sake, that he might make his mighty power to be known. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: so he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> And he saved them from the hand of him that hated them, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> And the waters covered their enemies: there was not one of them left. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Then believed they his words; they sang his praise. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> They soon forgat his works; they waited not for his counsel:^[**106:13** They soon…: Heb. They made haste, they forgat] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and tempted God in the desert.^[**106:14** lusted…: Heb. lusted a lust] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> And he gave them their request; but sent leanness into their soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> They envied Moses also in the camp, and Aaron the saint of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the company of Abiram. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> They made a calf in Horeb, and worshipped the molten image. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> They forgat God their saviour, which had done great things in Egypt; <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> Wondrous works in the land of Ham, and terrible things by the Red sea. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> Yea, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his word:^[**106:24** the pleasant…: Heb. a land of desire] <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> But murmured in their tents, and hearkened not unto the voice of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them in the wilderness:^[**106:26** to overthrow: Heb. to make them fall] <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter them in the lands.^[**106:27** To overthrow: Heb. To make them fall] <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> They joined themselves also unto Baal-peor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions: and the plague brake in upon them. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and so the plague was stayed. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> And that was counted unto him for righteousness unto all generations for evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> They angered him also at the waters of strife, so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes: <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spake unadvisedly with his lips. <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the LORD commanded them: <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works. <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> And they served their idols: which were a snare unto them. <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto devils, <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> And shed innocent blood, even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: and the land was polluted with blood. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went a whoring with their own inventions. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> Therefore was the wrath of the LORD kindled against his people, insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance. <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that hated them ruled over them. <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection under their hand. <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked him with their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.^[**106:43** brought…: or, impoverished, or, weakened] <sup class='bibleverse'>44</sup> Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their cry: <sup class='bibleverse'>45</sup> And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies. <sup class='bibleverse'>46</sup> He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them captives. <sup class='bibleverse'>47</sup> Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from among the heathen, to give thanks unto thy holy name, and to triumph in thy praise. <sup class='bibleverse'>48</sup> Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the LORD.^[**106:48** Praise…: Heb. Hallelujah]







 

# 107 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O give thanks unto the LORD, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy; <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the west, from the north, and from the south.^[**107:3** south: Heb. sea] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no city to dwell in. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he delivered them out of their distresses. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul with goodness. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, being bound in affliction and iron; <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned the counsel of the most High: <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; they fell down, and there was none to help. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saved them out of their distresses. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and brake their bands in sunder. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron in sunder. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Fools because of their transgression, and because of their iniquities, are afflicted. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; and they draw near unto the gates of death. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saveth them out of their distresses. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered them from their destructions. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his works with rejoicing.^[**107:22** rejoicing: Heb. singing] <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business in great waters; <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> These see the works of the LORD, and his wonders in the deep. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth up the waves thereof.^[**107:25** raiseth: Heb. maketh to stand] <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: their soul is melted because of trouble. <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wits’ end. ^[**107:27** are…: Heb. all their wisdom is swallowed up] <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he bringeth them out of their distresses. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves thereof are still. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> Then are they glad because they be quiet; so he bringeth them unto their desired haven. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and praise him in the assembly of the elders. <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the watersprings into dry ground; <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein.^[**107:34** barrenness: Heb. saltiness] <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground into watersprings. <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation; <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits of increase. <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and suffereth not their cattle to decrease. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> Again, they are minished and brought low through oppression, affliction, and sorrow. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in the wilderness, where there is no way.^[**107:40** wilderness: or, void place] <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, and maketh him families like a flock.^[**107:41** from: or, after] <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> The righteous shall see it, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall stop her mouth. <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> Whoso is wise, and will observe these things, even they shall understand the lovingkindness of the LORD.






 

# 108 
A Song or Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O God, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> I will praise thee, O LORD, among the people: and I will sing praises unto thee among the nations. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth reacheth unto the clouds.^[**108:4** clouds: or, skies] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth; <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> That thy beloved may be delivered: save with thy right hand, and answer me. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength of mine head; Judah is my lawgiver; <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over Philistia will I triumph. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom? <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our hosts? <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Give us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Through God we shall do valiantly: for he it is that shall tread down our enemies.
 

# 109 
To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise; <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue.^[**109:2** of the deceitful: Heb. of deceit]^[**109:2** are opened: Heb. have opened themselves] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> They compassed me about also with words of hatred; and fought against me without a cause. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For my love they are my adversaries: but I give myself unto prayer. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right hand.^[**109:6** Satan: or, an adversary] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his prayer become sin.^[**109:7** be condemned: Heb. go out guilty, or, wicked] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Let his days be few; and let another take his office.^[**109:8** office: or, charge] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them seek their bread also out of their desolate places. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let the strangers spoil his labour. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: neither let there be any to favour his fatherless children. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Let his posterity be cut off; and in the generation following let their name be blotted out. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD; and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Let them be before the LORD continually, that he may cut off the memory of them from the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, but persecuted the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: as he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.^[**109:18** into his bowels: Heb. within him] <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Let it be unto him as the garment which covereth him, and for a girdle wherewith he is girded continually. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Let this be the reward of mine adversaries from the LORD, and of them that speak evil against my soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name’s sake: because thy mercy is good, deliver thou me. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> For I am poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of fatness. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> I became also a reproach unto them: when they looked upon me they shaked their heads. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> Help me, O LORD my God: O save me according to thy mercy: <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> That they may know that this is thy hand; that thou, LORD, hast done it. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth; yea, I will praise him among the multitude. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, to save him from those that condemn his soul.^[**109:31** those…: Heb. the judges of]






 

# 110 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> The LORD said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thine enemies thy footstool. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The LORD shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule thou in the midst of thine enemies. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, in the beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: thou hast the dew of thy youth.^[**110:3** from…: or, more than the womb of the morning: thou shalt have, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The LORD hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The Lord at thy right hand shall strike through kings in the day of his wrath. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill the places with the dead bodies; he shall wound the heads over many countries.^[**110:6** many: or, great] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He shall drink of the brook in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head.

 

# 111 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. I will praise the LORD with my whole heart, in the assembly of the upright, and in the congregation.^[**111:1** Praise ye…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The works of the LORD are great, sought out of all them that have pleasure therein. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> His work is honourable and glorious: and his righteousness endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the LORD is gracious and full of compassion. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> He hath given meat unto them that fear him: he will ever be mindful of his covenant.^[**111:5** meat: Heb. prey] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> He hath shewed his people the power of his works, that he may give them the heritage of the heathen. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> The works of his hands are verity and judgment; all his commandments are sure. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> They stand fast for ever and ever, and are done in truth and uprightness.^[**111:8** stand…: Heb. are established] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He sent redemption unto his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever: holy and reverend is his name. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom: a good understanding have all they that do his commandments: his praise endureth for ever.^[**111:10** a good…: or, good success]^[**111:10** his commandments: Heb. them]




 

# 112 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Blessed is the man that feareth the LORD, that delighteth greatly in his commandments.^[**112:1** Praise…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the upright shall be blessed. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Wealth and riches shall be in his house: and his righteousness endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: he is gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: he will guide his affairs with discretion.^[**112:5** discretion: Heb. judgment] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed, trusting in the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> His heart is established, he shall not be afraid, until he see his desire upon his enemies. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honour. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The wicked shall see it, and be grieved; he shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish.

 

# 113 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Praise, O ye servants of the LORD, praise the name of the LORD.^[**113:1** Praise ye…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Blessed be the name of the LORD from this time forth and for evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same the LORD’s name is to be praised. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The LORD is high above all nations, and his glory above the heavens. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Who is like unto the LORD our God, who dwelleth on high,^[**113:5** dwelleth…: Heb. exalteth himself to dwell] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Who humbleth himself to behold the things that are in heaven, and in the earth! <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He raiseth up the poor out of the dust, and lifteth the needy out of the dunghill; <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> That he may set him with princes, even with the princes of his people. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He maketh the barren woman to keep house, and to be a joyful mother of children. Praise ye the LORD.^[**113:9** to keep…: Heb. to dwell in an house]


 

# 114 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of strange language; <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Judah was his sanctuary, and Israel his dominion. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The sea saw it, and fled: Jordan was driven back. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The mountains skipped like rams, and the little hills like lambs. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou Jordan, that thou wast driven back? <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams; and ye little hills, like lambs? <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob; <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Which turned the rock into a standing water, the flint into a fountain of waters. 

# 115 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Not unto us, O LORD, not unto us, but unto thy name give glory, for thy mercy, and for thy truth’s sake. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is now their God? <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> But our God is in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he hath pleased. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Their idols are silver and gold, the work of men’s hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they see not: <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they smell not: <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they walk not: neither speak they through their throat. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> They that make them are like unto them; so is every one that trusteth in them. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> O Israel, trust thou in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Ye that fear the LORD, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> The LORD hath been mindful of us: he will bless us; he will bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> He will bless them that fear the LORD, both small and great.^[**115:13** and: Heb. with] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> The LORD shall increase you more and more, you and your children. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Ye are blessed of the LORD which made heaven and earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD’s: but the earth hath he given to the children of men. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> The dead praise not the LORD, neither any that go down into silence. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> But we will bless the LORD from this time forth and for evermore. Praise the LORD.
 

# 116 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I love the LORD, because he hath heard my voice and my supplications. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Because he hath inclined his ear unto me, therefore will I call upon him as long as I live.^[**116:2** as long…: Heb. in my days] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The sorrows of death compassed me, and the pains of hell gat hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.^[**116:3** gat…: Heb. found me] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Then called I upon the name of the LORD; O LORD, I beseech thee, deliver my soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Gracious is the LORD, and righteous; yea, our God is merciful. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The LORD preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Return unto thy rest, O my soul; for the LORD hath dealt bountifully with thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from tears, and my feet from falling. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted: <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> I said in my haste, All men are liars. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> What shall I render unto the LORD for all his benefits toward me? <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of his saints. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> O LORD, truly I am thy servant; I am thy servant, and the son of thine handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will call upon the name of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people, <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> In the courts of the LORD’s house, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD.

 

# 117 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O praise the LORD, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> For his merciful kindness is great toward us: and the truth of the LORD endureth for ever. Praise ye the LORD. 

# 118 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: because his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let Israel now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Let them now that fear the LORD say, that his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I called upon the LORD in distress: the LORD answered me, and set me in a large place.^[**118:5** in distress: Heb. out of distress] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The LORD is on my side; I will not fear: what can man do unto me?^[**118:6** on…: Heb. for me] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> The LORD taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall I see my desire upon them that hate me. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in man. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in princes. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> All nations compassed me about: but in the name of the LORD will I destroy them.^[**118:10** destroy…: Heb. cut them off] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: but in the name of the LORD I will destroy them. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> They compassed me about like bees; they are quenched as the fire of thorns: for in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.^[**118:12** destroy: Heb. cut down] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: but the LORD helped me. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> The LORD is my strength and song, and is become my salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> The right hand of the LORD is exalted: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> The LORD hath chastened me sore: but he hath not given me over unto death. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, and I will praise the LORD: <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> This gate of the LORD, into which the righteous shall enter. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> The stone which the builders refused is become the head stone of the corner. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> This is the LORD’s doing; it is marvellous in our eyes.^[**118:23** the LORD’s…: Heb. from the LORD] <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> This is the day which the LORD hath made; we will rejoice and be glad in it. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> Save now, I beseech thee, O LORD: O LORD, I beseech thee, send now prosperity. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the LORD: we have blessed you out of the house of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> God is the LORD, which hath shewed us light: bind the sacrifice with cords, even unto the horns of the altar. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, I will exalt thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.




 

## 
# 119 
א ALEPH. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the LORD.^[**119:1** undefiled: or, perfect, or, sincere] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Blessed are they that keep his testimonies, and that seek him with the whole heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Thou hast commanded us to keep thy precepts diligently. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes! <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned thy righteous judgments.^[**119:7** thy…: Heb. judgments of thy righteousness] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.

 ## 
ב BETH. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed thereto according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Thy word have I hid in mine heart, that I might not sin against thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Blessed art thou, O LORD: teach me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as much as in all riches. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect unto thy ways. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word. ## 
ג GIMEL. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> Deal bountifully with thy servant, that I may live, and keep thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law.^[**119:18** Open: Heb. Reveal] <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> I am a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from me. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> My soul breaketh for the longing that it hath unto thy judgments at all times. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Thou hast rebuked the proud that are cursed, which do err from thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Princes also did sit and speak against me: but thy servant did meditate in thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> Thy testimonies also are my delight and my counsellors.^[**119:24** my counsellors: Heb. men of my counsel]

 ## 
ד DALETH. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken thou me according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>27</sup> Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk of thy wondrous works. <sup class='bibleverse'>28</sup> My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according unto thy word.^[**119:28** melteth: Heb. droppeth] <sup class='bibleverse'>29</sup> Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law graciously. <sup class='bibleverse'>30</sup> I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid before me. <sup class='bibleverse'>31</sup> I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O LORD, put me not to shame. <sup class='bibleverse'>32</sup> I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge my heart. ## 
ה HE. <sup class='bibleverse'>33</sup> Teach me, O LORD, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it unto the end. <sup class='bibleverse'>34</sup> Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yea, I shall observe it with my whole heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>35</sup> Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for therein do I delight. <sup class='bibleverse'>36</sup> Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to covetousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>37</sup> Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; and quicken thou me in thy way.^[**119:37** Turn…: Heb. Make to pass] <sup class='bibleverse'>38</sup> Stablish thy word unto thy servant, who is devoted to thy fear. <sup class='bibleverse'>39</sup> Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments are good. <sup class='bibleverse'>40</sup> Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy righteousness. ## 
ו VAU. <sup class='bibleverse'>41</sup> Let thy mercies come also unto me, O LORD, even thy salvation, according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>42</sup> So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me: for I trust in thy word.^[**119:42** So…: or, So shall I answer him that reproveth me in a thing] <sup class='bibleverse'>43</sup> And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I have hoped in thy judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>44</sup> So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>45</sup> And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts.^[**119:45** at liberty: Heb. at large] <sup class='bibleverse'>46</sup> I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not be ashamed. <sup class='bibleverse'>47</sup> And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have loved. <sup class='bibleverse'>48</sup> My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes.

 ## 
ז ZAIN. <sup class='bibleverse'>49</sup> Remember the word unto thy servant, upon which thou hast caused me to hope. <sup class='bibleverse'>50</sup> This is my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath quickened me. <sup class='bibleverse'>51</sup> The proud have had me greatly in derision: yet have I not declined from thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>52</sup> I remembered thy judgments of old, O LORD; and have comforted myself. <sup class='bibleverse'>53</sup> Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that forsake thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>54</sup> Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage. <sup class='bibleverse'>55</sup> I have remembered thy name, O LORD, in the night, and have kept thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>56</sup> This I had, because I kept thy precepts. ## 
ח CHETH. <sup class='bibleverse'>57</sup> Thou art my portion, O LORD: I have said that I would keep thy words. <sup class='bibleverse'>58</sup> I intreated thy favour with my whole heart: be merciful unto me according to thy word.^[**119:58** favour: Heb. face] <sup class='bibleverse'>59</sup> I thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>60</sup> I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>61</sup> The bands of the wicked have robbed me: but I have not forgotten thy law.^[**119:61** bands: or, companies] <sup class='bibleverse'>62</sup> At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee because of thy righteous judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>63</sup> I am a companion of all them that fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>64</sup> The earth, O LORD, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes. 
## 
ט TETH. <sup class='bibleverse'>65</sup> Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O LORD, according unto thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>66</sup> Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>67</sup> Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>68</sup> Thou art good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>69</sup> The proud have forged a lie against me: but I will keep thy precepts with my whole heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>70</sup> Their heart is as fat as grease; but I delight in thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>71</sup> It is good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might learn thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>72</sup> The law of thy mouth is better unto me than thousands of gold and silver. ## 
י JOD. <sup class='bibleverse'>73</sup> Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>74</sup> They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I have hoped in thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>75</sup> I know, O LORD, that thy judgments are right, and that thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me.^[**119:75** right: Heb. righteousness] <sup class='bibleverse'>76</sup> Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant.^[**119:76** for…: Heb. to comfort me] <sup class='bibleverse'>77</sup> Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: for thy law is my delight. <sup class='bibleverse'>78</sup> Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: but I will meditate in thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>79</sup> Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that have known thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>80</sup> Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I be not ashamed. 
## 
כ CAPH. <sup class='bibleverse'>81</sup> My soul fainteth for thy salvation: but I hope in thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>82</sup> Mine eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me? <sup class='bibleverse'>83</sup> For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; yet do I not forget thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>84</sup> How many are the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me? <sup class='bibleverse'>85</sup> The proud have digged pits for me, which are not after thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>86</sup> All thy commandments are faithful: they persecute me wrongfully; help thou me.^[**119:86** faithful: Heb. faithfulness] <sup class='bibleverse'>87</sup> They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>88</sup> Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; so shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth. ## 
ל LAMED. <sup class='bibleverse'>89</sup> For ever, O LORD, thy word is settled in heaven. <sup class='bibleverse'>90</sup> Thy faithfulness is unto all generations: thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.^[**119:90** unto…: Heb. to generation and generation]^[**119:90** abideth: Heb. standeth] <sup class='bibleverse'>91</sup> They continue this day according to thine ordinances: for all are thy servants. <sup class='bibleverse'>92</sup> Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction. <sup class='bibleverse'>93</sup> I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast quickened me. <sup class='bibleverse'>94</sup> I am thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>95</sup> The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I will consider thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>96</sup> I have seen an end of all perfection: but thy commandment is exceeding broad.

 ## 
מ MEM. <sup class='bibleverse'>97</sup> O how love I thy law! it is my meditation all the day. <sup class='bibleverse'>98</sup> Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine enemies: for they are ever with me.^[**119:98** they…: Heb. it is ever with me] <sup class='bibleverse'>99</sup> I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy testimonies are my meditation. <sup class='bibleverse'>100</sup> I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>101</sup> I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might keep thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>102</sup> I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught me. <sup class='bibleverse'>103</sup> How sweet are thy words unto my taste! yea, sweeter than honey to my mouth!^[**119:103** taste: Heb. palate] <sup class='bibleverse'>104</sup> Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate every false way.

 ## 
נ NUN. <sup class='bibleverse'>105</sup> Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path.^[**119:105** lamp: or, candle] <sup class='bibleverse'>106</sup> I have sworn, and I will perform it, that I will keep thy righteous judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>107</sup> I am afflicted very much: quicken me, O LORD, according unto thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>108</sup> Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O LORD, and teach me thy judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>109</sup> My soul is continually in my hand: yet do I not forget thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>110</sup> The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>111</sup> Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they are the rejoicing of my heart. <sup class='bibleverse'>112</sup> I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes alway, even unto the end.^[**119:112** to perform: Heb. to do]

 ## 
ס SAMECH. <sup class='bibleverse'>113</sup> I hate vain thoughts: but thy law do I love. <sup class='bibleverse'>114</sup> Thou art my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>115</sup> Depart from me, ye evildoers: for I will keep the commandments of my God. <sup class='bibleverse'>116</sup> Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: and let me not be ashamed of my hope. <sup class='bibleverse'>117</sup> Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect unto thy statutes continually. <sup class='bibleverse'>118</sup> Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: for their deceit is falsehood. <sup class='bibleverse'>119</sup> Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth like dross: therefore I love thy testimonies.^[**119:119** puttest…: Heb. causest to cease] <sup class='bibleverse'>120</sup> My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy judgments. ## 
ע AIN. <sup class='bibleverse'>121</sup> I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to mine oppressors. <sup class='bibleverse'>122</sup> Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress me. <sup class='bibleverse'>123</sup> Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy righteousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>124</sup> Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, and teach me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>125</sup> I am thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>126</sup> It is time for thee, LORD, to work: for they have made void thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>127</sup> Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yea, above fine gold. <sup class='bibleverse'>128</sup> Therefore I esteem all thy precepts concerning all things to be right; and I hate every false way. ## 
פ PE. <sup class='bibleverse'>129</sup> Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep them. <sup class='bibleverse'>130</sup> The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth understanding unto the simple. <sup class='bibleverse'>131</sup> I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>132</sup> Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, as thou usest to do unto those that love thy name.^[**119:132** as thou…: Heb. according to the custom toward those, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>133</sup> Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have dominion over me. <sup class='bibleverse'>134</sup> Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>135</sup> Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; and teach me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>136</sup> Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, because they keep not thy law. ## 
צ TZADDI. <sup class='bibleverse'>137</sup> Righteous art thou, O LORD, and upright are thy judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>138</sup> Thy testimonies that thou hast commanded are righteous and very faithful.^[**119:138** righteous: Heb. righteousness]^[**119:138** faithful: Heb. faithfulness] <sup class='bibleverse'>139</sup> My zeal hath consumed me, because mine enemies have forgotten thy words.^[**119:139** consumed…: Heb. cut me off] <sup class='bibleverse'>140</sup> Thy word is very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it.^[**119:140** pure: Heb. tried, or, refined] <sup class='bibleverse'>141</sup> I am small and despised: yet do not I forget thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>142</sup> Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, and thy law is the truth. <sup class='bibleverse'>143</sup> Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: yet thy commandments are my delights.^[**119:143** taken…: Heb. found me] <sup class='bibleverse'>144</sup> The righteousness of thy testimonies is everlasting: give me understanding, and I shall live. 



## 
ק KOPH. <sup class='bibleverse'>145</sup> I cried with my whole heart; hear me, O LORD: I will keep thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>146</sup> I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.^[**119:146** and I…: or, that I may keep] <sup class='bibleverse'>147</sup> I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>148</sup> Mine eyes prevent the night watches, that I might meditate in thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>149</sup> Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O LORD, quicken me according to thy judgment. <sup class='bibleverse'>150</sup> They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>151</sup> Thou art near, O LORD; and all thy commandments are truth. <sup class='bibleverse'>152</sup> Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast founded them for ever. ## 
ר RESH. <sup class='bibleverse'>153</sup> Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget thy law. <sup class='bibleverse'>154</sup> Plead my cause, and deliver me: quicken me according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>155</sup> Salvation is far from the wicked: for they seek not thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>156</sup> Great are thy tender mercies, O LORD: quicken me according to thy judgments.^[**119:156** Great: or, Many] <sup class='bibleverse'>157</sup> Many are my persecutors and mine enemies; yet do I not decline from thy testimonies. <sup class='bibleverse'>158</sup> I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept not thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>159</sup> Consider how I love thy precepts: quicken me, O LORD, according to thy lovingkindness. <sup class='bibleverse'>160</sup> Thy word is true from the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments endureth for ever.^[**119:160** Thy word…: Heb. The beginning of thy word is true]

 ## 
ש SCHIN. <sup class='bibleverse'>161</sup> Princes have persecuted me without a cause: but my heart standeth in awe of thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>162</sup> I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil. <sup class='bibleverse'>163</sup> I hate and abhor lying: but thy law do I love. <sup class='bibleverse'>164</sup> Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy righteous judgments. <sup class='bibleverse'>165</sup> Great peace have they which love thy law: and nothing shall offend them.^[**119:165** nothing…: Heb. they shall have no stumblingblock] <sup class='bibleverse'>166</sup> LORD, I have hoped for thy salvation, and done thy commandments. <sup class='bibleverse'>167</sup> My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them exceedingly. <sup class='bibleverse'>168</sup> I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways are before thee. ## 
ת TAU. <sup class='bibleverse'>169</sup> Let my cry come near before thee, O LORD: give me understanding according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>170</sup> Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to thy word. <sup class='bibleverse'>171</sup> My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy statutes. <sup class='bibleverse'>172</sup> My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments are righteousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>173</sup> Let thine hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts. <sup class='bibleverse'>174</sup> I have longed for thy salvation, O LORD; and thy law is my delight. <sup class='bibleverse'>175</sup> Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy judgments help me. <sup class='bibleverse'>176</sup> I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I do not forget thy commandments. 

# 120 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> In my distress I cried unto the LORD, and he heard me. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips, and from a deceitful tongue. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?^[**120:3** What shall be given…: or, What shall the deceitful tongue give unto thee? or, what shall is profit thee?]^[**120:3** done: Heb. added] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.^[**120:4** Sharp…: or, It is as the sharp arrows of the mighty man, with coals of juniper] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, that I dwell in the tents of Kedar! <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> I am for peace: but when I speak, they are for war.^[**120:7** for peace: or, a man of peace]



 

# 121 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.^[**121:1** I will…: or, Shall I lift up mine eyes to the hills? whence should my help come?] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.
 

# 122 
A Song of degrees of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Jerusalem is builded as a city that is compact together: <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, unto the testimony of Israel, to give thanks unto the name of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house of David.^[**122:5** are…: Heb. do sit] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Peace be within thy walls, and prosperity within thy palaces. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> For my brethren and companions’ sakes, I will now say, Peace be within thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Because of the house of the LORD our God I will seek thy good.
 

# 123 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Behold, as the eyes of servants look unto the hand of their masters, and as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; so our eyes wait upon the LORD our God, until that he have mercy upon us. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Have mercy upon us, O LORD, have mercy upon us: for we are exceedingly filled with contempt. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, and with the contempt of the proud. 

# 124 
A Song of degrees of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, now may Israel say; <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, when men rose up against us: <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Then they had swallowed us up quick, when their wrath was kindled against us: <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Then the waters had overwhelmed us, the stream had gone over our soul: <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Then the proud waters had gone over our soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Blessed be the LORD, who hath not given us as a prey to their teeth. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers: the snare is broken, and we are escaped. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Our help is in the name of the LORD, who made heaven and earth. 

# 125 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> They that trust in the LORD shall be as mount Zion, which cannot be removed, but abideth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> As the mountains are round about Jerusalem, so the LORD is round about his people from henceforth even for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.^[**125:3** the wicked: Heb. wickedness] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Do good, O LORD, unto those that be good, and to them that are upright in their hearts. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the LORD shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: but peace shall be upon Israel.
 

# 126 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> When the LORD turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like them that dream.^[**126:1** turned…: Heb. returned the returning] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with singing: then said they among the heathen, The LORD hath done great things for them.^[**126:2** hath…: Heb. hath magnified to do with them] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The LORD hath done great things for us; whereof we are glad. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Turn again our captivity, O LORD, as the streams in the south. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.^[**126:5** joy: or, singing] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves with him.^[**126:6** precious…: or, seed basket]



 

# 127 
A Song of degrees for Solomon. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Except the LORD build the house, they labour in vain that build it: except the LORD keep the city, the watchman waketh but in vain.^[**127:1** for…: or, of Solomon]^[**127:1** that…: Heb. that are builders of it in it] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> It is vain for you to rise up early, to sit up late, to eat the bread of sorrows: for so he giveth his beloved sleep. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Lo, children are an heritage of the LORD: and the fruit of the womb is his reward. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> As arrows are in the hand of a mighty man; so are children of the youth. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Happy is the man that hath his quiver full of them: they shall not be ashamed, but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate.^[**127:5** his…: Heb. filled his quiver with them]^[**127:5** speak…: or, subdue, or, destroy]



 

# 128 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Blessed is every one that feareth the LORD; that walketh in his ways. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> For thou shalt eat the labour of thine hands: happy shalt thou be, and it shall be well with thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Thy wife shall be as a fruitful vine by the sides of thine house: thy children like olive plants round about thy table. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Behold, that thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The LORD shall bless thee out of Zion: and thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Yea, thou shalt see thy children’s children, and peace upon Israel. 

# 129 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth, may Israel now say:^[**129:1** Many…: or, Much] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth: yet they have not prevailed against me.^[**129:2** Many…: or, Much] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> The plowers plowed upon my back: they made long their furrows. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> The LORD is righteous: he hath cut asunder the cords of the wicked. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Zion. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Let them be as the grass upon the housetops, which withereth afore it groweth up: <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Wherewith the mower filleth not his hand; nor he that bindeth sheaves his bosom. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Neither do they which go by say, The blessing of the LORD be upon you: we bless you in the name of the LORD.

 

# 130 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Out of the depths have I cried unto thee, O LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Lord, hear my voice: let thine ears be attentive to the voice of my supplications. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> If thou, LORD, shouldest mark iniquities, O Lord, who shall stand? <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> But there is forgiveness with thee, that thou mayest be feared. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I wait for the LORD, my soul doth wait, and in his word do I hope. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> My soul waiteth for the Lord more than they that watch for the morning: I say, more than they that watch for the morning.^[**130:6** I say…: or, which watch unto] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Let Israel hope in the LORD: for with the LORD there is mercy, and with him is plenteous redemption. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities.
 

# 131 
A Song of degrees of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> LORD, my heart is not haughty, nor mine eyes lofty: neither do I exercise myself in great matters, or in things too high for me.^[**131:1** exercise…: Heb. walk]^[**131:1** high: Heb. wonderful] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Surely I have behaved and quieted myself, as a child that is weaned of his mother: my soul is even as a weaned child.^[**131:2** myself: Heb. my soul] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Let Israel hope in the LORD from henceforth and for ever.^[**131:3** henceforth: Heb. now]



 

# 132 
A Song of degrees. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> LORD, remember David, and all his afflictions: <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> How he sware unto the LORD, and vowed unto the mighty God of Jacob; <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house, nor go up into my bed; <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> I will not give sleep to mine eyes, or slumber to mine eyelids, <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Until I find out a place for the LORD, an habitation for the mighty God of Jacob.^[**132:5** an habitation: Heb. habitations] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: we found it in the fields of the wood. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> We will go into his tabernacles: we will worship at his footstool. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Arise, O LORD, into thy rest; thou, and the ark of thy strength. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; and let thy saints shout for joy. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> For thy servant David’s sake turn not away the face of thine anointed. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> The LORD hath sworn in truth unto David; he will not turn from it; Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy throne.^[**132:11** body: Heb. belly] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I shall teach them, their children shall also sit upon thy throne for evermore. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> For the LORD hath chosen Zion; he hath desired it for his habitation. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> This is my rest for ever: here will I dwell; for I have desired it. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor with bread.^[**132:15** abundantly: or, surely] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> I will also clothe her priests with salvation: and her saints shall shout aloud for joy. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> There will I make the horn of David to bud: I have ordained a lamp for mine anointed.^[**132:17** lamp: or, candle] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> His enemies will I clothe with shame: but upon himself shall his crown flourish.



 

# 133

# 135 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. for the LORD is good: sing praises unto his name; for it is pleasant. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For the LORD hath chosen Jacob unto himself, and Israel for his peculiar treasure. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> For I know that the LORD is great, and that our Lord is above all gods. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Whatsoever the LORD pleased, that did he in heaven, and in earth, in the seas, and all deep places. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> He causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; he maketh lightnings for the rain; he bringeth the wind out of his treasuries. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, both of man and beast.^[**135:8** both…: Heb. from man unto beast] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Who sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt, upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings; <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and all the kingdoms of Canaan: <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> And gave their land for an heritage, an heritage unto Israel his people. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thy name, O LORD, endureth for ever; and thy memorial, O LORD, throughout all generations.^[**135:13** throughout…: Heb. to generation and generation] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> For the LORD will judge his people, and he will repent himself concerning his servants. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, the work of men’s hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> They have mouths, but they speak not; eyes have they, but they see not; <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> They have ears, but they hear not; neither is there any breath in their mouths. <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> They that make them are like unto them: so is every one that trusteth in them. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Bless the LORD, O house of Israel: bless the LORD, O house of Aaron: <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> Bless the LORD, O house of Levi: ye that fear the LORD, bless the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, which dwelleth at Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD.

 

# 136 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> O give thanks unto the God of gods: for his mercy endureth
