his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Who remembered us in our low estate: for his mercy endureth for ever: <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> And hath redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>25</sup> Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy endureth for ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>26</sup> O give thanks unto the God of heaven: for his mercy endureth for ever.

 

# 137 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yea, we wept, when we remembered Zion. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> We hanged our harps upon the willows in the midst thereof. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For there they that carried us away captive required of us a song; and they that wasted us required of us mirth, saying, Sing us one of the songs of Zion.^[**137:3** a song: Heb. the words of a song]^[**137:3** wasted…: Heb. laid us on heaps] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> How shall we sing the LORD’s song in a strange land?^[**137:4** strange…: Heb. land of a stranger?] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand forget her cunning. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth; if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.^[**137:6** my chief…: Heb. the head of my joy] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Remember, O LORD, the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem; who said, Rase it, rase it, even to the foundation thereof.^[**137:7** Rase it: Heb. Make bare] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; happy shall he be, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us.^[**137:8** destroyed: Heb. wasted]^[**137:8** rewardeth…: Heb. recompenseth unto thee thy deed which thou didst to us] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Happy shall he be, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against the stones.^[**137:9** the stones: Heb. the rock]







 

# 138 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I will praise thee with my whole heart: before the gods will I sing praise unto thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> I will worship toward thy holy temple, and praise thy name for thy lovingkindness and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> In the day when I cried thou answeredst me, and strengthenedst me with strength in my soul. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O LORD, when they hear the words of thy mouth. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Yea, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD: for great is the glory of the LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Though the LORD be high, yet hath he respect unto the lowly: but the proud he knoweth afar off. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: thou shalt stretch forth thine hand against the wrath of mine enemies, and thy right hand shall save me. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> The LORD will perfect that which concerneth me: thy mercy, O LORD, endureth for ever: forsake not the works of thine own hands. 

# 139 
To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> O LORD, thou hast searched me, and known me. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou understandest my thought afar off. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted with all my ways.^[**139:3** compassest: or, winnowest] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For there is not a word in my tongue, but, lo, O LORD, thou knowest it altogether. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thine hand upon me. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Such knowledge is too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot attain unto it. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy presence? <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> If I ascend up into heaven, thou art there: if I make my bed in hell, behold, thou art there. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> If I take the wings of the morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea; <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall hold me. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night shall be light about me. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth as the day: the darkness and the light are both alike to thee.^[**139:12** hideth…: Heb. darkeneth not]^[**139:12** the darkness and…: Heb. as is the darkness, so is the light] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my mother’s womb. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> I will praise thee; for I am fearfully and wonderfully made: marvellous are thy works; and that my soul knoweth right well.^[**139:14** right…: Heb. greatly] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> My substance was not hid from thee, when I was made in secret, and curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.^[**139:15** substance: or, strength, or, body] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; and in thy book all my members were written, which in continuance were fashioned, when as yet there was none of them.^[**139:16** all…: Heb. all of them]^[**139:16** which…: or, what days they should be fashioned] <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! how great is the sum of them! <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> If I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: when I awake, I am still with thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me therefore, ye bloody men. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> For they speak against thee wickedly, and thine enemies take thy name in vain. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> Do not I hate them, O LORD, that hate thee? and am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee? <sup class='bibleverse'>22</sup> I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies. <sup class='bibleverse'>23</sup> Search me, O God, and know my heart: try me, and know my thoughts: <sup class='bibleverse'>24</sup> And see if there be any wicked way in me, and lead me in the way everlasting.^[**139:24** wicked…: Heb. way of pain, or, grief]







 

# 140 
To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Deliver me, O LORD, from the evil man: preserve me from the violent man;^[**140:1** violent…: Heb. man of violences] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Which imagine mischiefs in their heart; continually are they gathered together for war. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adders’ poison is under their lips. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Keep me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a net by the wayside; they have set gins for me. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I said unto the LORD, Thou art my God: hear the voice of my supplications, O LORD. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, thou hast covered my head in the day of battle. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked: further not his wicked device; lest they exalt themselves. Selah.^[**140:8** lest…: or, let them not be exalted] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> As for the head of those that compass me about, let the mischief of their own lips cover them. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Let burning coals fall upon them: let them be cast into the fire; into deep pits, that they rise not up again. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Let not an evil speaker be established in the earth: evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow him.^[**140:11** an…: or, an evil speaker (Heb. a man of tongue), a wicked man of violence, be established in the earth: let him be hunted to his overthrow] <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted, and the right of the poor. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Surely the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name: the upright shall dwell in thy presence.


 

# 141 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> LORD, I cry unto thee: make haste unto me; give ear unto my voice, when I cry unto thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let my prayer be set forth before thee as incense; and the lifting up of my hands as the evening sacrifice.^[**141:2** set…: Heb. directed] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Set a watch, O LORD, before my mouth; keep the door of my lips. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Incline not my heart to any evil thing, to practise wicked works with men that work iniquity: and let me not eat of their dainties. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Let the righteous smite me; it shall be a kindness: and let him reprove me; it shall be an excellent oil, which shall not break my head: for yet my prayer also shall be in their calamities.^[**141:5** me; it shall be a…: or, me kindly, and reprove me; let not their precious oil break, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> When their judges are overthrown in stony places, they shall hear my words; for they are sweet. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Our bones are scattered at the grave’s mouth, as when one cutteth and cleaveth wood upon the earth. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> But mine eyes are unto thee, O GOD the Lord: in thee is my trust; leave not my soul destitute.^[**141:8** leave…: Heb. make not my soul bare] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Keep me from the snares which they have laid for me, and the gins of the workers of iniquity. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst that I withal escape.^[**141:10** escape: Heb. pass over]



 

# 142 
Maschil of David; A Prayer when he was in the cave. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I cried unto the LORD with my voice; with my voice unto the LORD did I make my supplication.^[**142:1** Maschil…: or, A Psalm of David, giving instruction] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> I poured out my complaint before him; I shewed before him my trouble. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my path. In the way wherein I walked have they privily laid a snare for me. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> I looked on my right hand, and beheld, but there was no man that would know me: refuge failed me; no man cared for my soul.^[**142:4** I looked…: or, Look on the right hand, and see]^[**142:4** failed…: Heb. perished from me]^[**142:4** cared…: Heb. sought after] <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I cried unto thee, O LORD: I said, Thou art my refuge and my portion in the land of the living. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Attend unto my cry; for I am brought very low: deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the righteous shall compass me about; for thou shalt deal bountifully with me.



 

# 143 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Hear my prayer, O LORD, give ear to my supplications: in thy faithfulness answer me, and in thy righteousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight shall no man living be justified. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me is desolate. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> I stretch forth my hands unto thee: my soul thirsteth after thee, as a thirsty land. Selah. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Hear me speedily, O LORD: my spirit faileth: hide not thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.^[**143:7** lest…: or, for I am become like, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Cause me to hear thy lovingkindness in the morning; for in thee do I trust: cause me to know the way wherein I should walk; for I lift up my soul unto thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Deliver me, O LORD, from mine enemies: I flee unto thee to hide me.^[**143:9** flee…: Heb. hide me with thee] <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: thy spirit is good; lead me into the land of uprightness. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Quicken me, O LORD, for thy name’s sake: for thy righteousness’ sake bring my soul out of trouble. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, and destroy all them that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant.

 

# 144 
A Psalm of David. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Blessed be the LORD my strength, which teacheth my hands to war, and my fingers to fight:^[**144:1** strength: Heb. rock]^[**144:1** to war…: Heb. to the war, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> My goodness, and my fortress; my high tower, and my deliverer; my shield, and he in whom I trust; who subdueth my people under me.^[**144:2** My goodness: or, My mercy] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> LORD, what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him! or the son of man, that thou makest account of him! <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Man is like to vanity: his days are as a shadow that passeth away. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Bow thy heavens, O LORD, and come down: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: shoot out thine arrows, and destroy them. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Send thine hand from above; rid me, and deliver me out of great waters, from the hand of strange children;^[**144:7** hand from: Heb. hands from] <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> I will sing a new song unto thee, O God: upon a psaltery and an instrument of ten strings will I sing praises unto thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> It is he that giveth salvation unto kings: who delivereth David his servant from the hurtful sword.^[**144:10** salvation: or, victory] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood: <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth; that our daughters may be as corner stones, polished after the similitude of a palace:^[**144:12** polished: Heb. cut] <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> That our garners may be full, affording all manner of store: that our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets:^[**144:13** all…: Heb. from kind to kind] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> That our oxen may be strong to labour; that there be no breaking in, nor going out; that there be no complaining in our streets.^[**144:14** strong…: Heb. able to bear burdens, or, loaden with flesh] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> Happy is that people, that is in such a case: yea, happy is that people, whose God is the LORD.







 

# 145 
David’s Psalm of praise. <sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness is unsearchable.^[**145:3** and his…: Heb. and of his greatness there is no search] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works.^[**145:5** works: Heb. things, or, words] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness.^[**145:6** declare: Heb. declare it] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness. <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy.^[**145:8** of great…: Heb. great in mercy] <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> The LORD is good to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD; and thy saints shall bless thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power; <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations.^[**145:13** an…: Heb. a kingdom of all ages] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> The LORD upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all those that be bowed down. <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat in due season.^[**145:15** wait…: or, look unto] <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living thing. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works.^[**145:17** holy: or, merciful, or, bountiful] <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> The LORD is nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them. <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> The LORD preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy. <sup class='bibleverse'>21</sup> My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.






 

# 146 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Praise the LORD, O my soul.^[**146:1** Praise ye…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> While I live will I praise the LORD: I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, in whom there is no help.^[**146:3** help: or, salvation] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the LORD his God: <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein is: which keepeth truth for ever: <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners: <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: the LORD raiseth them that are bowed down: the LORD loveth the righteous: <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> The LORD preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> The LORD shall reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, unto all generations. Praise ye the LORD.

 

# 147 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD: for it is good to sing praises unto our God; for it is pleasant; and praise is comely. <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> The LORD doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.^[**147:3** wounds: Heb. griefs] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by their names. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding is infinite.^[**147:5** his…: Heb. of his understanding there is no number] <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> The LORD lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Sing unto the LORD with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp unto our God: <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains. <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> He giveth to the beast his food, and to the young ravens which cry. <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man. <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy. <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion. <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee. <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He maketh peace in thy borders, and filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.^[**147:14** He…: Heb. Who maketh thy border peace]^[**147:14** finest…: Heb. fat of wheat] <sup class='bibleverse'>15</sup> He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: his word runneth very swiftly. <sup class='bibleverse'>16</sup> He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes. <sup class='bibleverse'>17</sup> He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold? <sup class='bibleverse'>18</sup> He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, and the waters flow. <sup class='bibleverse'>19</sup> He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments unto Israel.^[**147:19** his word: Heb. his words] <sup class='bibleverse'>20</sup> He hath not dealt so with any nation: and as for his judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD.




 

# 148 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: praise him in the heights.^[**148:1** Praise ye the LORD. Praise: Heb. Hallelujah, etc] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light. <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that be above the heavens. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Let them praise the name of the LORD: for he commanded, and they were created. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass. <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps: <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> Fire, and hail; snow, and vapour; stormy wind fulfilling his word: <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars: <sup class='bibleverse'>10</sup> Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:^[**148:10** flying…: Heb. birds of wing] <sup class='bibleverse'>11</sup> Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth: <sup class='bibleverse'>12</sup> Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children: <sup class='bibleverse'>13</sup> Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven.^[**148:13** excellent: Heb. exalted] <sup class='bibleverse'>14</sup> He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the LORD.


 

# 149 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his praise in the congregation of saints.^[**149:1** Praise…: Heb. Hallelujah] <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.^[**149:2** in him…: Heb. in his Makers] <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.^[**149:3** in…: or, with the pipe] <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation. <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, and a twoedged sword in their hand;^[**149:6** mouth: Heb. throat] <sup class='bibleverse'>7</sup> To execute vengeance upon the heathen, and punishments upon the people; <sup class='bibleverse'>8</sup> To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron; <sup class='bibleverse'>9</sup> To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all his saints. Praise ye the LORD.



 

# 150 
<sup class='bibleverse'>1</sup> Praise ye the LORD. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power.+ 150.1 Praise ye…: Heb. Hallelujah <sup class='bibleverse'>2</sup> Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness. <sup class='bibleverse'>3</sup> Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp.+ 150.3 trumpet: or, cornet <sup class='bibleverse'>4</sup> Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs.+ 150.4 dance: or, pipe <sup class='bibleverse'>5</sup> Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals. <sup class='bibleverse'>6</sup> Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD. Praise ye the LORD.
